  <script>
   function generateUUID() {
        let d = new Date().getTime();
        const uuid = 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function (c) {
          const r = (d + Math.random() * 16) % 16 | 0;
          d = Math.floor(d / 16);
          return (c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x7) | 0x8).toString(16);
        });
        return uuid;
      };

      var eventData = [
        'key=web.preload.loaded',
        'clientType=web',
        'url=' + window.location.href,
        'value={"appName":"next"}',
        'app=phoenix',
        'screenSize=' + '{"height":' + window.innerHeight + ', "width":' + window.innerWidth + '}',
        'clientVersion=' + (window.coursera && window.coursera.config && window.coursera.config.version) || '',
        'clientTimestamp=' + Date.now(),
        'visitId=' + generateUUID(),
        'guid=' + generateUUID()
      ];

      var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
      request.open('POST', 'https://www.coursera.org/eventing/info.v2');
      request.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
      request.send(encodeURI(eventData.join('&')));
  </script>
